❞✐✈✐❞✐❞♦ ❡♠ q✉❛❞r❛❞✐♥❤♦s ✉♥✐tÆr✐♦s✳ ▼❛rq✉❡ ♦s ♣♦♥t♦s q✉❡ sª♦ ✈Ørt✐❝❡s ❞❡ ❛❧❣✉♠

♣♦ss❡ ❞❛ ✜❣✉r❛ ♥♦ t❛❜✉❧❡✐r♦✱ ✉♠❛ ♣❛rt❡ ❞♦s ❛❧✉♥♦s ❛✐♥❞❛ t✐✈❡r❛♠ ❞✐✜❝✉❧❞❛❞❡ ♣❛r❛ ✐❞❡♥✲
t✐✜❝❛r q✉❡♠ s❡r✐❛ ♦ mdc(10, 15) ❡ ♦ mmc(10, 15)✳ ❆♣(cid:243)s ❛❧❣✉♥s ✐♥st❛♥t❡s ♦❜s❡r✈❛♥❞♦✱
❝❤❡❣❛r❛♠ (cid:224) ❝♦♥❝❧✉sª♦ ❞❡ q✉❡ ❛ ❞✐❛❣♦♥❛❧ ✭❡❧Æst✐❝♦ ✈❡r♠❡❧❤♦✮ ✜❝♦✉ ❞✐✈✐❞✐❞❛ ❡♠ 5 ♣❛rt❡s
❡ q✉❡✱ ❡♠ ❝❛❞❛ ✉♠ ❞♦s r❡t(cid:226)♥❣✉❧♦s ❞❡t❡r♠✐♥❛❞♦s✱ ❡①✐st✐❛♠ 30 q✉❛❞r❛❞✐♥❤♦s❀ ❡♥tª♦✱

❋✐❣✉r❛ ✸✳✼✿ ❈Æ❧❝✉❧♦ ❞❡ ♠♠❝ ❡ ♠❞❝ ❞♦ 10 ❡ 15

♣r✐♠❡✐r♦✱ ❝♦♥t✐♥✉❛♠♦s ❝♦♠ ♦ ❝Æ❧❝✉❧♦ ❞♦ ♠♠❝ ❡ ♠❞❝ ❛tr❛✈Øs ❞♦ t❛❜✉❧❡✐r♦✱ ❥Æ ✈✐st♦ ♥❛

♠♠❝ ❞❡ ❞♦✐s ♥œ♠❡r♦s✳ ◆❛ ♠❛✐♦r✐❛ ❞❡❧❡s✱ ❢♦r❛♠ ♦s ❛❧✉♥♦s q✉❡ ♣❡♥s❛✈❛♠ ❡ ❝♦♥str✉(cid:237)❛♠ ♦s

5 ❡ 7✱ ❝♦♥str✉(cid:237)❞♦ ♣♦r ✉♠❛ ❛❧✉♥❛✳

◆❡st❡ ❡①❡♠♣❧♦✱ t✐✈❡♠♦s ❛❧❣✉♠❛s ❞✐✜❝✉❧❞❛❞❡ ♣❛r❛ ❞❡t❡r♠✐♥❛r t❛♥t♦ ♦ ♠❞❝ q✉❛♥t♦
♦ ♠♠❝✳ ❆ ♠❛✐♦r✐❛ ❞♦s ❛❧✉♥♦s✱ q✉❛♥❞♦ ♣❡r❣✉♥t❛♠♦s q✉❡♠ s❡r✐❛♠ ♦ mdc(5, 7) ❡ ♦

❞♦ ♣r♦❝❡❞✐♠❡♥t♦✳ ❊♠ s❡❣✉✐♥❞❛✱ ✈♦❧t❛♠♦s ❛ ♦❜s❡r✈❛r ♦ r❡t(cid:226)♥❣✉❧♦✲♣r♦❜❧❡♠❛ ♥♦ t❛❜✉✲

mdc(5, 7) = 1✳

❈♦♠♦ ❥Æ t✐♥❤❛♠♦s ❡♥❝♦♥tr❛❞♦ ♦ ♠❞❝✱ ❛ ♠❛✐♦r ♣❛rt❡ ❞❛ t✉r♠❛ ❛❝❤❛✈❛ q✉❡ ♦ mmc(5, 7)
t❛♠❜Ø♠ s❡r✐❛ 1✳ ▼❛✐s ✉♠❛ ✈❡③✱ ✈♦❧t❛♠♦s ❛ ❢❛③❡r ❛ ❧❡✐t✉r❛ ❞♦ t❡①t♦ q✉❡ ❢❛❧❛ ❝♦♠♦ ❡♥✲

q✉❛❞r❛❞✐♥❤♦s ❡①✐st❡♥t❡s ♥♦ r❡t(cid:226)♥❣✉❧♦ ❞❡ ❧❛❞♦s 5 ❡ 7✳ ❆ss✐♠✱ ✜❝♦✉ ❝♦♠♣r❡❡♥❞✐❞♦ q✉❡ ♦

♠❛✐s s❡ ♣r❛t✐❝❛✱ ♠❛✐s s❡ ❛♣r❡♥❞❡✱ ❞❡✐①❛♠♦s✱ ♠❛✐s ✉♠❛ ✈❡③✱ ♦s ❛❧✉♥♦s ❡①❡❝✐t❛r❡♠ ♦s

❆♦ ✜♥❛❧ ❞❡ss❡ ♠♦♠❡♥t♦✱ ❝♦♠♣r❡❡♥❞❡✲s❡ q✉❡ ✈Ær✐❛s ✐♥t❡r♣r❡t❛(cid:231)ı❡s ♣♦❞❡♠ s❡r ✉t✐❧✐✲

♦ ♠❞❝ ❡ ♠♠❝ sª♦ ❞❡ ❝✉♥❤♦ ❡ss❡♥❝✐❛❧♠❡♥t❡ ❛r✐t♠Øt✐❝♦✱ ♣♦rt❛♥t♦ ♣♦❞❡♠ s❡r ✐♥t❡r♣r❡t❛❞♦s

♥♦ss❛s ❛✉❧❛s✿ ♦ ❥♦❣♦ ❞❛s tr✐❧❤❛s✱ q✉❡ t❡♠ ❝♦♠♦ ♦❜❥❡t✐✈♦ ♦ ❛♣r✐♠♦r❛♠❡♥t♦ ❞♦ ❝Æ❧❝✉❧♦
